    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Experteam, kurulduğu 2000 yılından bugüne kadar iş uygulamaları ve bilgi teknolojileri konularında hizmet vermektedir.  Experteam, gerçekleştirilen proje sayısı, sağladığı uzman hizmetler, danışman sayısı, geniş çözüm portföyü ve uzmanlığı en büyük çözüm ortaklarından birisidir. Experteam, Oracle tarafından Türkiye’deki en üst seviye olan Platinum Partner seviyesinde sınıflandırılmaktadır.

Experteam’in artarak devam eden başarısının temelinde çözüm üreten, akılcı, çalışkan ve müşteri memnuniyeti odaklı çalışma ilkeleri yatmaktadır.

Experteam, proje bitimini takiben, müşterilerinin yaşayan sistemlerinin gereği olan kesintisiz, verimli ve kaliteli bakım hizmetlerini, ISO 27001 Bilgi Güvenliği sertifikasına sahip olan Experteam Yönetilen Hizmetler (EYM) üzerinden ITIL hizmet yönetimi süreçlerine uygun olarak sunmaktadır.
          </p>

          <dl class="mt-6">
              
    <div class="mb-2 flex papabear:mr-3 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:flex-wrap" data-test-id="about-us__website">
      <dt class="font-sans text-md font-bold text-color-text break-words w-40 papabear:flex-shrink-0 papabear:mr-3 mamabear:flex-shrink-0 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:mb-1">
          Web Sitesi
      </dt>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌍 Finance &amp; IT Leaders Meet in Istanbul!

We are excited to announce the upcoming Istanbul Finance &amp; IT Roundtable, taking place on September 17th at Conrad Hotel, Istanbul.

Together with our partner <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/splash-bi?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SplashBI</a>, we will showcase how Oracle EBS and Fusion users can streamline their financial reporting processes. We are also pleased to welcome <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/rishabh-miglani?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Rishabh Miglani</a> and <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/marc-mcgurk?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Marc McGurk</a> from SplashBI, who will be joining us from London and sharing their expertise. The sessions will cover:

Transitioning from Oracle Discoverer to modern reporting tools
Solutions to common reporting challenges faced by Finance &amp; IT teams
Live demos of GLConnect, SQL Connect, and SplashBI

This roundtable will be a unique opportunity for CFOs, IT leaders, ERP managers, and reporting professionals to connect, exchange ideas, and explore innovative solutions.

📍 Date: September 17, 2025
📍 Venue: Conrad Hotel, Istanbul

Registration : <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dhs9a2ra?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dhs9a2ra</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Last week, we had the privilege of bringing together industry leaders at Çırağan Palace for an inspiring event focused on driving digital innovation in the Construction and Engineering sector, in collaboration with our valued vendor, Oracle.
 
Throughout the event, we presented how Oracle Fusion Cloud ERP, powered by embedded AI, is transforming HR, finance, supply chain, and project management. With AI-driven insights, this platform empowers companies to forecast with pinpoint accuracy, optimize resources, improve safety, and accelerate sustainable project delivery—redefining efficiency across every department.
 
At Experteam, we are proud to combine Oracle’s global innovation with our industry-specific expertise, empowering construction companies to adopt digital transformation strategies that unlock greater efficiency, agility, and long-term success.
 
We extend our sincere thanks to all the forward-thinking professionals who joined us. This is just the beginning—together, we are building the digital future of construction.
